for the infants and toddlers to connect with each other and their caregivers. It also provides opportunities to enhance their language and gross motor skills.</p></div></div></div></div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_blurb et_pb_blurb_6  et_pb_text_align_left  et_pb_blurb_position_left et_pb_bg_layout_light et_pb_blurb_position_top_phone"><div class="et_pb_blurb_content"><div class="et_pb_main_blurb_image"><span class="et_pb_image_wrap"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="91" height="91" src="https://7oaks.sg/ps/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/Group-4594-1.png" alt="" srcset="https://7oaks.sg/ps/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/Group-4594-1.png 91w, https://7oaks.sg/ps/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/Group-4594-1-75x75.png 75w" sizes="(max-width: 91px) 100vw, 91px" class="et-waypoint et_pb_animation_top et_pb_animation_top_tablet et_pb_animation_top_phone wp-image-1660"></span></div><div class="et_pb_blurb_container"><h4 class="et_pb_module_header"><span>Outdoor play</span></h4><div class="et_pb_blurb_description"><p>We promote outdoor learning for our children. Playing outdoors allow infants to learn about different surroundings and enabling them to feel more comfortable with the world around them. As for toddlers, they are more keen to test out their growing physical skills.</p></div></div></div></div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_blurb et_pb_blurb_7  et_pb_text_align_left  et_pb_blurb_position_left et_pb_bg_layout_light et_pb_blurb_position_top_phone"><div class="et_pb_blurb_content"><div class="et_pb_main_blurb_image"><span class="et_pb_image_wrap"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="91" height="90" src="https://7oaks.sg/ps/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/Group-4593-1.png" alt="" srcset="https://7oaks.sg/ps/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/Group-4593-1.png 91w, https://7oaks.sg/ps/wp-content/uploads/2021/10/Group-4593-1-75x75.png 75w" sizes="(max-width: 91px) 100vw, 91px" class="et-waypoint et_pb_animation_top et_pb_animation_top_tablet et_pb_animation_top_phone wp-image-1661"></span></div><div class="et_pb_blurb_container"><h4 class="et_pb_module_header"><span>Bonding time</span></h4><div class="et_pb_blurb_description"><p>Infants in our care get lots of one-on-one time with their educarors. about our infant care</h2></div></div></div></div><div class="et_pb_row et_pb_row_16"><div class="et_pb_column et_pb_column_4_4 et_pb_column_29  et_pb_css_mix_blend_mode_passthrough et-last-child"><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_43 et_animated  et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light" data-animation-style="fade" data-animation-repeat="" data-animation-duration="1000ms" data-animation-delay="0ms" data-animation-intensity="50%" data-animation-starting-opacity="0%" data-animation-speed-curve="ease-in-out"><div class="et_pb_text_inner"><div class="strong-view strong-view-id-5 modern wpmtst-modern slider-container slider-mode-fade slider-adaptive controls-type-sides controls-style-buttons2" data-count="3" data-slider-var="strong_slider_id_5" data-state="init"><div class="wpmslider-wrapper" style="max-width: 100%;"><div class="wpmslider-viewport" aria-live="polite" style="width: 100%; overflow: hidden; position: relative; height: 439.625px;"><div class="strong-content wpmslider-content" style="width: auto; position: relative;"><div class="wpmtst-testimonial testimonial t-slide post-891" style="float: none; list-style: none; position: absolute; width: 623px; z-index: 50; display: block; height: auto;" aria-hidden="false"><div class="wpmtst-testimonial-inner testimonial-inner"><div data-infinite-loop="false" class="wpmtst-testimonial-content  testimonial-content"><div><strong align="center" class="name-testi">Mdm Su’aidah</strong><p></p><div align="center" class="from-testi">Mother of Haris<br> from Infant Care, PPIS Child Development Care Centre Sembawang</div></div><p>“Being a working mum and first-time parent, entrusting a stranger to care for my baby wasn’t easy for me. I experienced a separation anxiety and constantly worried if my son is in good hands or not. As days and months passed, I could see how smiley and excited he gets when he sees the teachers every morning. I know that he’s gotten all the love from the teachers. I could not have asked for anything more than that. Because I know that he is well taken care off.”</p></div><div class="clear"></div></div></div><div class="wpmtst-testimonial testimonial t-slide post-1252" style="float: none; list-style: none; position: absolute; width: 623px; z-index: 0; display: none; height: auto;" aria-hidden="true"><div class="wpmtst-testimonial-inner testimonial-inner"><div data-infinite-loop="false" class="wpmtst-testimonial-content  testimonial-content"><div><strong align="center" class="name-testi">Mdm Khairun Nisa</strong><p></p><div align="center" class="from-testi">Mother of Ilyas Fahd from Infant Care, 7oaks Preschool – Sembawang</div></div><p>“When I had my second son, there is no doubt that I will send him to PPIS Infant Care.</p><p>With the pleasant experience I had with my first son, Adam…I could see that he has developed so much since he joined PPIS infant care in 2018. Now 2 years later, he still enjoys school and learning new things at PPIS Childcare Sembawang.”</p></div><div class="clear"></div></div></div><div class="wpmtst-testimonial testimonial t-slide post-1253" style="float: none; list-style: none; position: absolute; width: 623px; z-index: 0; display: none; height: auto;" aria-hidden="true"><div class="wpmtst-testimonial-inner testimonial-inner"><div data-infinite-loop="false" class="wpmtst-testimonial-content  testimonial-content"><div><strong align="center" class="name-testi">Parent of Mysha Alea</strong><p></p><div align="center" class="from-testi">from Infant Care, 7oaks Preschool – Bedok Reservoir</div></div><p>“It warms our heart to see our daughter smile widely at the infant care educarers when we send her to the centre every day. The main caregiver for my daughter is friendly and often update us about my daughter progress at dismissal time.</p><p>My daughter has a sensitive skin and her main caregiver recommended on different products that I could try on her. Alhamdullilah, my daughter skin condition has improved tremendously using the recommended product and under their care.”</p></div><div class="clear"></div></div></div></div></div><div
